### Drama Structure (simple + useful for *Woyzeck*)
When we analyze **Drama Structure**, weâ€™re not counting chapters. Weâ€™re looking at **how the conflict and tension develop over time**:
- **Exposition/Start**: Who is involved? Whatâ€™s the situation?
- **Rising action**: Pressure builds (more conflicts, humiliations, problems).
- **Turning point / climax**: A key moment changes everything (often a discovery/decision).
- **Falling action**: Consequences start rolling.
- **End**: Outcome (often tragic in *Woyzeck*).

In *Woyzeck*, because itâ€™s made of short scenes, it can feel like fragments â€” so tracking **pressure â†’ turn â†’ consequences** helps a lot.
